Chinese Businesses Report Closures After the Shenyang Incident

▲ More Than 400 Businesses Closed

▲ Losses Around 1.5 Million Yuan

Shenyang Correspondence: In recent years, although this city has been affected by the sharp rise in global gold prices, the municipal authorities have made every effort to promote construction and gradually develop plans, so business can still be maintained. Unexpectedly, after the occupying Shenyang by the violent army on September 18, it has been directly and indirectly affected, resulting in rising prices and hesitant customers, resulting in unbearable losses. The number of businesses that have declared closure is unprecedented since the city's founding. Yesterday, in order to find out the exact number, the reporter personally went to various businesses inside and outside the city to investigate. According to a Mr. Ji of Ji Shun Silk Shop's conversation in the Chamber of Commerce, from November 19 to December 5, more than 400 businesses have closed, with losses of about 1.5 million yuan.

From De Shun Tai Hardware Store outside Daxi Bianmen to Guandong Ginseng Shop inside the city, a total of 81 businesses of all sizes have closed, with losses of more than 500,000 yuan. The most prosperous Siping Street in the city, from Gulou to Zhonglou, has a total of 31 closures, including six large silk shops (i.e., silk and satin shops), with losses of more than 200,000 yuan. North of Gulou, except for the Commercial Press, Zhonghua Painting Bureau, and the four major painting bureaus of the world and Dadong, which are still operating normally, the remaining bookstores of all sizes have been closed for many days. From inside Xiaoxi Bianmen to inside Xiaodongmen, there are a total of more than 70 grocery stores, with losses of more than 300,000 yuan. From inside Dananmen to inside Dabeimen, there are more than 50 closures, with losses of more than 400,000 yuan. There are also more than 100 small shops, with a total loss of about 100,000 yuan. There are 12 grain stores and oil presses, which are completely stationed by Japanese soldiers. Lumber yards, money shops, and hotels are not included. If the situation remains the same in the future, there will be even more shops that continue to close due to unsustainability by the end of the lunar year.

French Troops Increase on the Sino-Vietnamese Border Situation

▲ French Troops Focus on Yunnan Province

▲ Total Troop Increase Nearly 20,000

Guangzhou Correspondence: The fact that the French government in Vietnam has increased its troops on the Yunnan-Guangxi border has become an undeniable fact. The following is an investigation into the deployment of French troops on the Sino-Vietnamese border and the recent troop increase situation, for the reference of Chinese people studying the Sino-Vietnamese border defense issue. It is found that Southern Vietnam is connected to Siam, and Northern Vietnam is connected to the Yunnan-Guangxi border of our country. The Vietnamese French government divides the border defense of this district into five routes. Each route is stationed with an infantry regiment. Lang Son Province is one route, with two battalions of Vietnamese troops stationed, numbering about 1,000 people, and about 300 French troops. Na Ling is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops and about 100 French troops. Qi Xi is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops and about 200 French troops. Cao Ping Province is one route, with Cao Ping stationed with about 1,000 Vietnamese troops and about 500 French troops. Dong Xi is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops and about 200 French troops. Na Long Tun (connected to Longzhou, Shuikou, etc. in Guangxi) is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops, Na Ling (Longbang in Guangxi) is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops, and Shuo Jiang (Pingmengyi in Guangxi) is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops. The above is connected to our Guangxi Province. He Yang Province is one route, with He Yang stationed with about 2,000 Vietnamese troops and about 500 French troops. You Wang (connected to Zhenmaguan) is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops, Tongfu is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops, Bao Le (connected to Tianpeng) is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops, and Fu Lao (connected to Jiu Dong) is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops. Lao Kai Province is one route, with Gu Le (connected to the Hekou of Yunnan) stationed with about 2,000 Vietnamese troops and about 500 French troops, Huangzhou Fei is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops and about 200 French troops, and Bu Cha (connected to Manhao) is stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops. The above is connected to our Yunnan Province. Hai Ning Province is one route, with Mang Jie (connected to Dongxing) stationed with about 500 Vietnamese troops and about 170 French troops, Xin Fan is stationed with about 150 Vietnamese troops and about 80 French troops, Bei Feng Tian is stationed with about 150 Vietnamese troops and about 70 French troops, and Ping Liao is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops and about 70 French troops. The above is connected to our Guangdong Province, Dongxing Fangcheng. Na Shu is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops and about 80 French troops. Ding Li is stationed with about 350 Vietnamese troops and about 100 French troops. He Qiang is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops and about 80 French troops. Xin An is stationed with about 300 Vietnamese troops and about 150 French troops. Other provinces such as Hai Phong, Hanoi, and Thanh Hoa are also heavily garrisoned. As for the organization of its troops, each infantry regiment is usually a three-battalion, four-company system. Each battalion has about 500 men. A regiment is attached to one machine gun company, one cavalry company, one artillery company, one engineer company, and one transportation company. Vietnam is a conscription system, but it also has recruitment. Among the French troops (Vietnamese natives generally called "Western troops"), there are also African black troops, numbering about 5,000. Li Yang troops (Vietnamese native language means "rogue," actually composed of rogues from various countries recruited by the Vietnamese government) number about 6,000. The real number of French troops is about 3,000. However, the number of Vietnamese troops conscripted nationwide, combined with the reserve service of 15 years, 20 years, etc., is about 1.5 million. The number of Miao and Yao ethnic minority troops recruited is also about 20,000. The troops increased this time include about 5,000 African black troops, about 10,000 newly recruited Vietnamese Miao and Yao ethnic minority troops, and about 2,000 Li Yang troops. The troop increase is most focused on Yunnan Province, followed by Guangxi Province. There is no increase on the Guangdong Province border. Only three new French warships have been added to Guangzhou Bay. The construction of airfields and the transportation of military supplies are extremely busy in Vietnam, and the situation is quite serious.

Hunan Province Increases Salt Tax to Fund Military Expenses

▲ Generals Propose Adding Three Yuan Per Package

▲ 2 Million Yuan Can Be Obtained Within Five Months

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province is originally a Huai salt import area. The price of salt was only seven or eight yuan per package ten years ago. Subsequently, military affairs were frequent. Zhao Hengti, Tang Shengzhi, and others repeatedly added special military donations to the salt tax, increasing it by one to four yuan each time. At the beginning of each donation increase, the number of tickets was limited, and it was stated that it would stop when the limit was reached. However, as a result, not only was it not canceled after the quota was filled, but it was repeatedly increased. In recent years, He Jian continued to collect taxes, and by the end of December 20, each package had been increased to 16 yuan and 6 jiao, of which the military expense surcharge accounted for more than eight or nine yuan. Therefore, the Hunan people bear the heaviest salt tax and pay the highest salt price for the Huai salt sold on the four banks of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi. The Fourth Route Army expenses of He Jian's troops are entirely dependent on this for maintenance. However, the troops stationed in Hunan include six divisions of He's troops, namely Wang Dongyuan, Peng Weiren, Li Jue, Tao Guang, Chen Guangzhong, and Chen Quzhen, plus one division of Sichuan troops, Zhang Ying, and part of Qian troops, Wang Chenglie. The monthly military expenses are about 1.5 million yuan. After He Jian returned to Hunan from Beijing a few days ago, he held a military conference to discuss ways to tighten military expenses. The minimum monthly requirement is 1 million yuan, and the income is only from salt tax, tobacco and alcohol, stamp duty, and cigarettes. In peak months, it can collect 1.12 million yuan, and in off-peak months, it only collects 700,000 to 800,000 yuan. Among them, the expenses of national tax agencies, the expenses of the Army Hospital and Surveying Bureau in Hunan, the funds allocated by the Salt Affairs Audit Office to repay foreign debts, and the 93,000 yuan allocated by the central government to Hunan Province for educational expenses each month, etc., total about 300,000 yuan, and are also included in this number. That is, the actual amount allocated to military expenses from the 1.12 million yuan collected in peak months is only 800,000 to 900,000 yuan, and only 400,000 to 500,000 yuan in off-peak months. Therefore, military expenses are extremely difficult, with arrears of up to ten months. The generals of each army then jointly discussed maintenance methods, and decided that increasing the salt tax was the most reliable. Therefore, five division commanders, including Wang Dongyuan, jointly requested He Jian to add three yuan per package to the Huai salt item, including the Ping Liu Xiu road fee, limited to 150 tickets. Each ticket is 4,000 packages, which can collect 12,000 yuan. 150 tickets can collect a total of 1.8 million yuan. In addition, refined salt, Sichuan salt, and Guangdong salt are also collected by comparison, which can collect more than 2 million yuan. Hunan can sell 30 tickets of salt per month, and 150 tickets can be sold out in five months. That is, the monthly salt tax revenue can be increased by 400,000 yuan. He Jian approved it and implemented it from January 1, 21st year. The collection method is appended as follows: (1) From January of the 20th year of the Republic of China, the number of military expenses and highways to be added is stipulated according to the various types of salt sold in the following areas, and the collection will be implemented. (A) The refined salt sold in Changyue Changtan and Si'an is subject to a military expense of 2.5 yuan per stone. (B) The Huaiyue salt sold in Baoqing and Hengyang is subject to a military expense of 1.5 yuan per stone and a highway donation of 3 jiao. (C) The Huaiyue salt sold in Jinshi, Yuanling, You County, and Qiyang is subject to a military expense of 1 yuan per stone and a highway donation of 2 jiao. (D) Hongjiang, Qianyang, Lingling, and Dong'an, regardless of Sichuan, Yue, or Huai salt, are subject to a military expense of 1 yuan per stone and are exempt from highway donations. (E) The Huai salt sold by other Huai salt bureaus is subject to a military expense of 2.5 yuan per stone and a highway donation of 5 jiao. (F) All Sichuan and Yue salt, regardless of water or drought, are subject to a military expense of 1 yuan per stone and are exempt from highway donations. (Note) The remaining jin of Huai salt are also collected in accordance with the regulations. (2) This military expense and highway donation shall be collected by the directors of each branch bureau and special bureau, who shall supervise the accounting and be responsible for the collection. They shall report and remit them to the general bureau in each district on a ten-day basis, and then remit them to the Fourth Route General Command and the provincial government for verification. The required remission fees shall be drawn from the remission money in accordance with the stipulated number of remission fees. However, the remission money and remission fees shall be clearly distinguished and shall not be confused in any way. In addition, if military pay is appropriated with printed receipts, no remission fees shall be paid. (3) Each bank bureau shall implement the collection from the date of receipt of the instruction and shall, on the date of receipt of the order, open a list of merchants and the number of dan of unsold salt in the warehouse and report it to the government for record. (4) All unsold salt in the warehouse, if it has been sold and a ticket has been issued, shall still be added in accordance with the regulations. (5) This military expense and highway donation shall be announced by each branch bureau and special bureau to the merchants and people to comply with and pay. Once the full amount has been collected, an order shall be issued to stop. (6) Each Sichuan and Yue salt tax bureau shall actively prevent the invasion of Huai salt import areas during the price increase period by using Yue salt jin and cheap Huai salt from neighboring provinces.

Details of the Suppression of Bandits in Huangpi

▲ Xu Tingyao Leads Two Brigades to Attack the Front of the Bandits

▲ The Bandits Retreat to Xinglongzui and Will Flee to the North Bank

Hankou Correspondence: The situation of the bandits attacking Huangpi County and requesting help has been reported in the previous letter. Today's news is indeed slightly eased. Initially, the bandits captured Huang'an and joined forces with the bandits in the northern township of Huangpi, intending to take advantage of the dissatisfaction of the government army to attack Huangpi County and advance south in a big way to disturb Wuhan. Unexpectedly, the two regiments of the Fourth Division's Xu Tingyao troops had arrived at the front line and tried their best to resist. Although there were many bandits, they were still mobs. Therefore, after contacting Xu's troops on the fourth and fifth days, they suffered many casualties, but they still tried their best to move forward and refused to retreat. At that time, the Xia Dingxin Brigade of the 13th Division's Xia Douyin troops stationed in Qijiawan was ordered to reinforce. Xia Brigade was the elite of the 13th Division, and the Queshan and Qufu battles were based on this brigade as the backbone (when Xia was a regiment commander under Lu Bentang). Since then, the addition of new troops to the battle made the bandit army even more unsustainable. When all the 11th and 12th Brigades of the Fourth Division arrived, Division Commander Xu Tingyao personally led the 11th Brigade Special Task Regiment and the Communication Battalion to the front to supervise the suppression. For a time, the morale was greatly boosted, and the people's hearts were greatly reassured. The bandit troops, with a large army gathered, found it difficult to attack the county seat, so they abandoned their original plan and wanted to advance south through the county seat. The purpose of the bandits was to achieve something else, not just to capture a city or occupy a place. However, the bandit's conspiracy was seen through by the government army early. After the armies were concentrated, they were deployed separately. The two brigades of Xu Tingyao's division were responsible for the frontal attack. The ninth team of armored vehicles was under Xu's command. The two regiments of Xia Douyin's division were responsible for the side attack. Xiao's division protected the railway, and Li's division guarded the county seat. After the deployment was completed, a large-scale suppression was launched. On the sixth and seventh days, Zhang Brigade of Xu's division and Xia Brigade of Xia's division had fierce battles with the bandit troops. At the same time, aircraft assisted, killing many bandits. Because the bandits suffered heavy losses, they retreated to the north on the morning of the eighth. The vanguard retreated to Xinglongzui, and the headquarters retreated to Yanzi Gang. The bandit army was exhausted and no longer dared to attack desperately. Division Commander Xu Tingyao, seeing that the bandits had been repelled, ordered his troops to follow up and suppress them, and sent Chief of Staff Sheng Shiheng to preside over the front. It is not yet certain whether he will return to Wuchang on the eighth to supervise the pursuit again. During the fierce battle between the soldiers and bandits, the Han Changjun Brigade of the 48th Division's Xu Yuanquan troops was also ordered to move from the Hebei district and the new district to ambush the bandits. The Luojiatian and other places have been recovered. On the eighth, Xu telegraphed to the Appeasement Office for a report. The original text is as follows: Hankou Appeasement Chief He Junjian, I learned that Brigadier Han Changjun of the Weiwu and Weishen telegrams, section said that six or seven hundred bandits fled near the mouth of the Yellow River and the new district. This morning, I ordered Regiment Commander Wang to lead the Yue Battalion, the Zong Regiment Zhang Battalion, and the Zhao Regiment Cao Battalion to advance to that area. I then received a report from Regiment Commander Wang, saying that the Yue Battalion advanced to two li from the mouth of the Yellow River and the new district at 9:00 am, encountering more than 200 bandits, half of whom had guns. After a fierce attack by our officers and soldiers, the bandits resisted slightly and fled to the Luojiatian area. At ten o'clock, the area was occupied. At the same time, Zhang Battalion advanced to near the Lilin shop, and a few bandits fled north at the sound of the wind. Cao Battalion advanced to near Zhangchangling, encountering more than 300 bandits, who were attacked by our Yue Battalion and fled to the Changyan area. After the troops searched and suppressed, they returned to their original defenses at 3:00 pm. There is no major change near Baliwan. Peng Brigade reported that the bandits of Dasheng Mountain were defeated. The 30th Division reported that the bandits were defeated in successive days. In addition to ordering the brigade to be vigilant and suppress them as appropriate, I hereby report. Xu Yuanquan bows, (January 8)

Lu Nan's Liu and Guo Divisions to Implement Reorganization

▲ Going to Gaotang from Dawenkou for Verification

Jinan Correspondence: Liu Guitang led his troops to surrender, and all arrangements have been thoroughly discussed and agreed upon. However, the date has been extended repeatedly, and the assembly is not yet complete. The reason is that Liu's troops are mostly within the Mengshan Mountains. He voluntarily agreed to transfer them completely for reorganization. Therefore, regarding the assembly time, the initial period was half a month, hoping that with a large number of people, a division could be formed. Han Fuju approved a period of ten days. Unexpectedly, after the deadline, he requested another extension because the number of people was still large and assembly required time. Zhan Shutang, commander of the 81st Division, came to Jinan from nearby to report to Han about this matter. According to Zhan, Liu Guitang and his troops are now in the area bordering Yishui and Mengyin, trying their best to avoid the army. There is still no news as to when the assembly will be completed. At that time, Han Fuju believed that Liu's troops had repeatedly violated the time limit for assembly, and it was urgent to inspect the truth. Therefore, he specially dispatched Liu Shuxiang, chief of the Staff Department, to Yanzhou for inspection and to discuss the issue of incorporating Liu's troops with Gu Liangmin, commander of the 21st Division stationed in Yanzhou. After Liu arrived in Yanzhou, Liu Guitang and Guo Mafeng repeatedly sent representatives to meet with Liu and Gu.

Page 12

They still claimed that the number of troops was too large and could not be assembled in a short period of time, and that many family members were being carried, which must be properly arranged. They requested that the assembly deadline be extended to before the 10th of this month, which was also approved by Han. As of yesterday (the 5th), the Provincial Government received another telegram from Liu Shuxiang and Gu Liangmin in Yanzhou reporting that Liu Guitang stated that in addition to urging the troops to assemble quickly, Liu himself would first lead his troops to Yishui for assembly, and Guo Mafeng's troops would also set off immediately. It was determined that they would be able to arrive for assembly before the 10th. Today (the 6th) in the afternoon, Han Fuju ordered the Railway Bureau to prepare a train of empty cars to depart for Dawenkou tomorrow. After Liu Guitang's troops assemble, they will board the train and be transported to the designated area in northern Shandong to await the dispatch of personnel for verification and reorganization. At the same time, the armored train "Beiping" was divided into two trains to patrol the Tianjin-Pukou and Jiaoji Railways. (6th)

Another report: The surrender and acceptance of Liu Guitang, Guo Mafeng, and other troops in southern Shandong. As a result of the contact between Liu Shuxiang, Gu Liangmin, and Liu Guitang's representative Xia Ziming, as of the 5th, Gu and Liu telegraphed that more than 4,000 troops of Liu and Guo had completed assembly and were scheduled to depart from Dabianqiao on foot to Dawenkou on the 7th to board the train. At the same time, he ordered Dai Hongbin, commander of the armored train, to divide the "Beiping" armored train into two trains to patrol and suppress the area between Dawenkou and Yucheng. (Liu's troops disembark at Yucheng and go to Gaotang) and telegraphed Gu Liangmin to be on strict alert at Dawenkou. As soon as Liu's troops arrive, they should board the train immediately, and only after arriving in Gaotang can they be verified and reorganized. However, those without guns are not allowed to board the train. Liu himself will also borrow Xia Ziming to come to Jinan and, together with Zhang Futian, who was sent by Shandong compatriots in Peiping to Jinan to handle this matter, pay respects to Han Fuju to discuss the reorganization procedures. The issue of incorporating Liu and Guo's troops can thus be concluded. Attached is the exchange of telegrams between Liu, Gu, and Han, as follows: 1. According to Deputy Officer Liu Donghan's telephone report from Bianqiao, Liu and Guo plan to lead their troops from Bianqiao to Dawenkou on Yu Day to await verification and reorganization. The number of people is approximately 4,000, and they need 10,000 steamed buns for supplies every day, etc. 3. In addition to dispatching Deputy Officer Liu Jizhong to Tai'an to coordinate with the County Government in handling all matters, and ordering the engineering battalion stationed in Tai'an and the forest regiment stationed in Sishui to be on strict guard, respectfully reported. To Master Gu of Yanzhou, Jing Xuan, First Director Liu, Wei Zhen brother: All five reports in Wei Wu's telegram have been received and understood. After Liu and Guo's troops arrive at Dawenkou, they should be ordered to board the train and go to Gaotang without verification to await verification and reorganization. However, those without firearms must not be allowed to board the train. This matter must be explained to Liu and Guo first. The required vehicles will be dispatched by the deputy officer on Yu Day and escorted to Dawenkou for use, and an armored train will be sent to provide security. However, at least a battalion-level unit must be dispatched in advance at Dawenkou Station to monitor closely to prevent unforeseen circumstances. Bandits Rob on the Road: On the evening of the 7th, Li Yuanru, who lived in Lou Tangzhen, was returning home by rickshaw after sitting in the city. While passing through the Heiyu area of Huangqing Township outside the North Gate, four bandits suddenly blocked the road, took out sharp blades, and forbade any noise. The rickshaw driver tried to escape to report to the police but was caught and severely beaten by the bandits. The bandits then took the stolen goods and fled into a small road.

Wuxi

Collection of Wine Tax: Farmers Petition. Farmers in the Huadafang Village area of the 13th District (i.e., Xin'an Township) in the county usually brew wine from mud wine and rotten wheat to serve as feed for pigs. The Wine License Tax Bureau has never collected taxes. Recently, Bao Luyi, the director of the Wine License Tax Collection Office, established a branch in Huada Village and collected wine tax from farmers, but it was inconsistent with the tax regulations. The day before yesterday, more than 700 farmers in the area, holding flags, set off on a parade to the 13th District Office to petition. The district chief, Zhu Zhengxin, received them. The representatives put forward four demands: 1. Reduce the public sales fee.

2. Stop illegal levies. 3. Immediately abolish the branch. 4. Severely punish Bao Luyi. District Chief Zhu agreed to submit a petition to the higher authorities for handling. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Also, the case of Huang Bingjian, a member of the 16th Branch, being bribed to exchange prisoners, is scheduled for a hearing on the 12th of this month. A formal letter was sent to the Public Security Bureau yesterday, ordering Huang Bingjian to be brought to the case for interrogation.

Education News

Important News

Advice from the Principal of Jiangsu Province to Students to Resume Classes (1)

The principals of Jiangsu Provincial Secondary Schools advise all secondary school students in the province to resume classes:

Our nation and people have suffered from the aggression and oppression of Western imperialists for a long time. In peacetime, economic aggression and cultural aggression are sufficient to control our fate. In times of trouble, political oppression and military oppression are used to the extreme. Anyone with blood and vigor can hardly bear this. Since our late Premier Sun Yat-sen advocated revolution, overthrew the Qing Dynasty, established the republic, and advocated fighting against imperialism and abolishing unequal treaties, people with imperialist tendencies have been thunderstruck and joined forces to go. The revolutionary forces have been vigorously promoted, and Western imperialists have become slightly more cautious. Unfortunately, in recent years, the sages of the party and the state have failed to uphold the late Premier's forty years of sacrifice and struggle, and to endure for the sake of the country, resulting in chaos. The facts are obvious and cannot be denied. Coupled with the natural disasters this year, the floods have caused suffering to the people. Thereupon, Japan, which has been coveting and plotting, has recognized this as a rare opportunity and has brazenly disregarded it and directly wielded the knife. Now, three provinces have fallen in just over three months, and the flames of war in the Northeast have spread throughout the country. People are at the mercy of the butcher's knife, and we are the fish and meat. China is in danger of being submerged, and the motherland is suffering from the pain of destruction. The first mistake was the authorities' policy of non-resistance, and the second mistake was the League of Nations' aiding the evildoers. The strong enemy took advantage of this, and the clowns became more rampant. Coupled with international conspiracies, which are treacherous and unpredictable, Yunnan and Guangxi are in alarm and are being forced to come together. Under this unprecedentedly serious situation, all the elderly know that they will soon die, and even if the country is destroyed and they become slaves and servants, they will not last long. However, they still gnash their teeth and speak out with righteous indignation, encouraging the remaining men, without looking back. Moreover, young students with rich emotions and surging blood, hearing the drums of the Northeast and seeing the rivers and mountains being swept away, are indignant, heartbroken, running around crying, and are forced to pick up their pens and rise up, strike, petition, propagandize, and raise donations. This is what they should do. The gentlemen of the universities took the lead, and the middle school students followed. They took the patriotism as the root and made empty calls. How can the youth fail the country? Although the vitality of the country lies in the youth, the youth's salvation of the country depends on their studies. Therefore, sacrificing the youth's studies is tantamount to destroying the vitality of the country. If the vitality remains, even if the country is destroyed, it can be expected to recover. If the vitality disappears, even if it survives, it will be difficult to avoid extinction. Therefore, striking and marching is to endure the pain for a while to urge the government and awaken the people, which is justice, conscience, and responsibility, and no one can criticize it. If the strike becomes long-term or indefinite, the marching, speeches, fundraising, and petitions will eventually be exhausted. Once the momentum is exhausted, it will decline again and again. As a result, laziness takes over, the country cannot be saved, and they are unwilling to study. The result is perfunctory, decadent, empty, and suicidal. No one dares to read it. Recently, Chiang Kai-shek resigned, the government was reorganized, and the previous rumors of neutrality in Jinzhou, joint management of Tianjin, and direct negotiations between China and Japan are no longer a problem. The youth's responsibility has been fulfilled, and the government's renewal can be expected. We send it out, and we can take it back. Therefore, for the sake of all the young gentlemen of secondary schools in our province, we should take this opportunity to regain our spirits, resume classes on a regular basis, and encourage and spur ourselves with the greatest determination and effort to progress in cultivating morality and undertaking studies, and to lie down on firewood and taste gall. The way to restore and cultivate the vitality of the country lies in this, and the way to fundamentally save the nation from danger also lies in this. Patriots must be able to love themselves, and those who save the country must first save themselves. Striving to cultivate personality is to love oneself, and striving to pursue knowledge and exercise the body is to save oneself. Apart from this, there is no other way. (To be continued)

Vow to Destroy Pirates: John Greatly Defeats Hujiang

32 to 23 points

A Fierce Battle at Xiqing Basketball Court

▲First Final in Group B

▲Huzhong Defeats Morning Star

The basketball elites of John's University and Hujiang University met at the Xiqing Basketball Room at 8:00 PM last night, with a fierce competition, neither side yielding. John's copper-walled defense made it difficult for Hujiang's generals, who usually hit every shot, to take even a step last night, and they succumbed to John's lead. The result was 22 to 23, a difference of nine points. John's hope for the Xiqing championship is more assured now. In the first final of Group B, the Hujiang Affiliated Middle School defeated the Morning Star team 31-24. There are still three more groups of second and third finals to be played. (1) Youtai defeated Meigong, B 1, 25-16. (2) Xiaguang defeated Qingguang, Group A 36-30. (3) Jinan defeated Dare to Die, Group A, 36-32.

John's Five Tigers Conquer Hujiang

▲Cheers Resounded, Each with Their Own Melody, Wonderfully Inexpressible Cheerleading Team Began Work The cheerleaders of both schools occupied the upper and lower floors of the deafening basketball room, and when John finally won, the joy was indescribable.

▲The Championship Is About John This match is greatly related to the championship. Although it was once severely poisoned by McLing, it is certainly able to overcome Hujiang, and can still compete with the pirates. The future is infinitely hopeful. However, it is difficult for Hujiang to defeat the pirates, and it will never be willing to be a female. Therefore, this battle is fierce. John Should Have Won Early John won by nine points. In terms of opportunity, it should not have reached this number. It could have been won much earlier. There were countless balls that were missed under the basket. The angle was only a little off, and it only needed to brush the board to go into the net, but it was missed. It's a pity that only two out of eleven free throws were made, which shows the problem. In the future, work should be done on this in the final against the pirates.

Copper Wall Iron Bastion

John's Victory: First, Steady and Calm Chen Xianglong and Cheng Jingshi are all able to strictly guard five people, forming a unified force that leaves Hujiang with no chance to shoot. Lin Zequn and Wu Youliang are like two tigers who never miss a shot. Hujiang ran into walls everywhere, while the forward Cheng Jingshi performed greatly, and therefore, victory was achieved.

Hujiang's Defeat

Hujiang's defeat was due to John's strict defense, and it cannot be denied that their performance was diminished. The workmen were flustered, playing the pipa wildly, committing fouls repeatedly, moving carefully with the ball, but unable to score. Feng Nianhua only scored three points, how could they not be defeated?

Smooth Sailing

John led all the way from the beginning to the end. Cheng Jingshi scored first, and Hujiang fought bravely, with the score only one or two points apart. At 6-5, 8-7, Yun Ruchun scored a long shot, making it 9-8, the only time Hujiang surpassed them. Hou Xuemin then scored three consecutive shots, giving John an 11-5 lead in the first half.

Retreating as a Strategy

After the break, Hujiang replaced Lin with Dai, adding three points suddenly. Feng Nianhua also scored, making it 16-14, and then 18-17, only one point behind. Hou Xuemin also added four points, and Hujiang fell behind again. John knew Hujiang's speed and used a delaying tactic against them, retreating as a strategy, not seeking to rush. Passing the ball right and left, Hujiang could do nothing. In the last minute, Lin Zequn scored a foul, making it 32-20 at the end of the game.

Vow to Destroy Pirates

The only strong enemy left for John is the pirates. Last night's victory over Hujiang greatly boosted morale, and they all resolved to vow to destroy the pirates.

Local News

Sun Ke Goes to Ningbo to Visit Chiang Today

Chiang, Hu, and Wang Must Actually Cooperate

Otherwise, Sun Also Indicates Resignation

Liu Luyin Went to Hong Kong Yesterday to See Hu

Amidst the national crisis, the call for Chiang, Hu, and Wang to jointly come to Beijing to preside over the central government has been resounding, but it has not yet materialized. A week after the new government was established, the Premier of the Executive Yuan, Sun Ke, expressed that he could not support it alone, so he came to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning and is scheduled to go to Fenghua today with Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng to visit Chiang and urge him to come. After Sun arrived in Shanghai yesterday, he intended to visit Wang Jingwei immediately, but Wang declined due to illness, only sending two representatives to visit Sun, informing him of the difficulty of not being able to meet due to illness. As for Hu Hanmin, who is recuperating in Hong Kong, Sun has also sent several telegrams urging him to come, but has received no reply. Feng Yuxiang also expressed yesterday that he would soon go to Hong Kong to visit Hu and to Ningbo to visit Chiang. Sun further told reporters that if he still cannot get one or two of the three gentlemen, Chiang, Hu, and Wang, to come to Beijing, then he will have to resign to apologize to the people of the country. The domestic and foreign troubles are so serious that the severity of the situation can be seen from this.

Important Speech by Sun Ke

Premier Sun gave a speech to reporters when he arrived in Shanghai yesterday, saying: "I came to Shanghai this time entrusted by my colleagues in the Central Committee to comfort Mr. Wang Jingwei and persuade him to dispel his intention to resign, recuperate peacefully, and come to Beijing as soon as possible. Moreover, the diplomatic issue now seems to have a new situation, but it can also be said to be a new difficulty. We must discuss it at length with Mr. Wang and others to obtain a proper response strategy. The current national environment is extremely difficult. I have repeatedly declared that the three gentlemen, Chiang, Hu, and Wang, must jointly come to Beijing to preside over the central government before there is a solution. I also plan to go to Fenghua within a few days to urge Mr. Chiang to return to Beijing immediately. As for whether it is possible for the three gentlemen, Chiang, Hu, and Wang, to jointly come to Beijing, I naturally cannot give a definite answer. However, the national crisis is so critical at the moment that the three gentlemen must come out together to bear the burden, which has become the unanimous demand of the entire party and the entire country. The purpose of my coming to Beijing this time is to promote the movement of sincere unity with the spirit of jointly facing the national crisis. I believe that this is a necessary path to save the country, so I will follow it regardless of all difficulties. The three gentlemen all have a long history in the party and the country, and in any case, they must not continue to ignore the crisis of the country and disregard it. I feel that my qualifications, reputation, and abilities are all shallow, and I am not capable of bearing the major responsibility of the Executive Yuan. However, I am not behind others in my love for the party and the country, and I especially cannot bear to see the Chinese Kuomintang and the Republic of China, which my late father worked so hard to create, gradually falling into a broken, fragmented, and irreparable danger. Since I have been entrusted by my comrades, I have no choice but to temporarily try my best to support the transitional situation, hoping to use my ability to promote the practical cooperation of the three gentlemen, Chiang, Wang, and Hu, and then I can be relieved of my responsibility. However, since I took office nine days ago, none of the three gentlemen has resolutely come to Beijing. This not only makes me personally distraught, but also makes the people of the whole country feel disappointed. The emptiness of the central government is the greatest danger to the country today. Those who have the power do not come to take responsibility, and I, who have no power, am forced to bear the greatest responsibility, which will inevitably lead to exhaustion and will not help the country. Seeing this danger, I cannot but make a most sincere request to the three gentlemen for the sake of the party and the country. If it is still not granted, then I have exhausted my wisdom and can only resign to avoid further delaying the time and harming the party and the country."

Yesterday Went to Moliai

Road, Sun's residence, to visit Premier Sun. Chen Mingshu, Wu Tiecheng, Xue Dubi, Li Zongren, and Li Jishen were present. At that time, Sun and the others discussed the current situation for a long time before they left.

After Detailed Discussion by the Executive and Supervisory Committee Members

The Strike Issue Was Considered a Major Matter

The Consent of All Industry Associations Must Be Solicited

Xin Sheng She reported that due to the loss of Jinzhou and the Japanese army's approach to Shanhaiguan, which is an emergency situation, and the government has no countermeasures, the Anti-Japanese Association of Shanghai Universities and the Anti-Japanese Association of Middle School Students requested a strike from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for four consecutive days from the fourth to the seventh of this month, and convened a citizens' assembly and a demonstration. The chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Wang Xiaolai, personally explained everything several times. Because the student representatives insisted on their request and their attitude was very angry, the Chamber of Commerce decided to convene an emergency meeting of the executive and supervisory committees for discussion at 4 pm yesterday after a standing committee meeting. More than 20 student representatives attended yesterday to explain the reasons and made sincere and earnest statements, and requested (1) a strike on Monday (2) a citizens' assembly to be held on the 17th, and asked for unanimous participation, etc. The executive and supervisory committee members who attended the meeting yesterday were Wang Xiaolai, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Yansong, Lu Qisheng, Chen Songyuan, Wu Zhihao, Cheng Xiechun, Gu Xinyi, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Wenqi, Pei Yunqing, Xiang Songmao, Jiang Zhigang, Lu Fengzhu, Ma Jiliang, Luo Qinghua, etc. discussed in detail and resolved that the executive and supervisory committee members expressed deep sympathy and admiration for the student representatives' patriotic enthusiasm. The request to participate in the citizens' assembly on the 17th, the association will notify all members to participate enthusiastically. Regarding the strike on Monday, although the executive and supervisory committee members can express their acceptance, but the matter is major and the consent of all industry associations must be solicited. The strike date is planned to be held on the 17th of this month.

Demobilization Loan Lottery Held Yesterday for Principal Repayment

Total Principal Repaid: $1,500,000

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the Ministry of Finance held the sixth principal repayment lottery for the Demobilization Loan at the Hong Kong Road Bankers' Association. Details are as follows:

Representatives present: Yang Tizhi from the Auditing Department as an inspector, Xu Jiqing from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Fan Jietang from the Fund Custody Committee, Hu Mengjia from the Shanghai Banking Association (representing Jin Jingyuan), Yan Junan from the Shanghai Money Trade Association, Li Yangsheng from the Central Bank as a lottery drawer, Cheng Muhao from the Bank of China, Wei Bo from the Bank of Communications, managers Lu Shutang, He Xiaojuan, Liang Yaozong, registrars Chen Shaochao, You Dunti, Chen Jian, clerical staff Huang Qizong, Xu Zuhuang, Huang Meizhao, and receptionists He Yaoqing, Zheng Yijian, Fang Jingzhong.

Chairman's Speech: Vice Minister of Finance Lin Kanghou presided and delivered a speech on behalf of Minister Huang, stating: "Today is the date for the sixth principal repayment lottery for the 18th Year Demobilization Loan. I am fortunate to be here with you all. The National Government has always been punctual in repaying principal and interest on all types of public bonds and treasury bills. In the year of 20 alone, over $114,680,000 was repaid in principal and over $57,250,000 in interest, totaling over $171,900,000. The credit of public bonds is extremely well-known. Recently, the bond market has declined slightly due to various reasons, mainly the trend of the financial market. The availability of credit is also related to the bond market. Currently, the government is striving to consolidate the original funds for all public bonds and treasury bills, and all monthly principal and interest payments will continue to be handled according to the original regulations without any changes. I believe the credit of public bonds and treasury bills will become more stable. This sixth lottery for the Demobilization Loan is the first of the 21st year. Being that it is closely watched, the Minister personally attends to show the importance we place on public bonds. In the future, we will continue to repay principal and interest on all types of public bonds and treasury bills on time. Directly maintaining public bonds is indirectly maintaining finance, and both should work together to transform the current economic situation. On the occasion of this lottery, I would like to clearly state the government's commitment to consolidating the credit of public bonds."

Lottery Report: Vice Minister Lin, substituting for the Minister, concluded his speech and reported: "Today is the date for the sixth principal repayment lottery for the 18th Year Demobilization Loan. We are delighted to have you all here to observe. The total value of the 18th Year Demobilization Loan issued was $50,000,000. Excluding the principal already repaid in the first to fifth lotteries, today's sixth repayment lottery will draw five lots, each for $500,000, totaling $2,500,000. All bond certificates drawn will be paid by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in all locations, starting from the 31st of this month, along with the sixth period interest, all paid in national currency, regardless of location. Please have the supervisors inspect the lottery lots and the lottery lot register for execution."

Winning Numbers: 06, 37, 78, 88, 98, a total of five lots. The total principal to be repaid is $2,500,000.

Merchant Steamship Company Strike Still Under Mediation

Hope for Resolution

Regarding the strike by Merchant Steamship Company sailors demanding wages, yesterday, mediators Du Yuesheng and Li Zhengwu were appointed to mediate, and one ship has already been sent out. The remaining ships are still suspended. The news from yesterday is summarized as follows:

Continuing Suspension of River Steamers: Twelve river and sea steamers have already been suspended. Yesterday, the Changjiang steamer "Jiangjing" also joined the strike after arriving in Shanghai and entering the port. Its sailors, stokers, etc., went to the union to automatically join the wage demand group and carried out the strike. If this is not resolved today, then the two steamers arriving in Shanghai today, "Jiangxin" and "Yushun," will also join. Other ships en route have sent telegrams to the association for inquiries and assistance.

Mediation Process: After Du and Li were appointed as mediators, the sailors and stokers nominated Jin Yueshi, Gong Wenfang, Che Defang, etc., to go to Du's residence to discuss the matter. The representatives stated the hardships of the employees on the ships, the meager wages, and that the monthly salary of sailors and stokers was only over $30, from which $12 was deducted for food. They even had to pay for their own soap, etc. How could the treatment compare with that of the bureau staff? Du and Li expressed great sympathy for the representatives' statements and promised to mediate.

First the Ningbo Route: Du and Li discussed with the representatives and said that they had contacted the bureau and would be responsible for resolving the issue of double wages. However, today, the "Xin Jiangtian" ship must first be sent to Ningbo from the thirteen suspended ships. The remaining ships will remain in Shanghai and wait quietly. If the problem cannot be resolved after the "Xin Jiangtian" sails, then the suspension can be resumed upon its return to Shanghai. The representatives decided to accept the proposal and issued a notice at 4:00 PM, allowing the "Xin Jiangtian" to resume sailing first. It departed at 5:30 PM. The meeting also issued a notice stating: "The issue of double wages for colleagues is now being negotiated by the representatives and mediators Mr. Du Yuesheng and Mr. Quanwu. There is no doubt about double wages, and they will be responsible for resolving it. It is hoped that the 'Xin Jiangtian' will be sent out first today. The remaining ships can wait quietly at the port. If a satisfactory resolution cannot be reached, the suspension can be resumed after the 'Xin Jiangtian' returns to Shanghai. Colleagues, in order to respect the opinions of the mediators, agree to allow the ship to sail today. Special notice."

Reporting to the Military Department: The association sent an urgent telegraph to the Military and Political Department yesterday, which was forwarded to the Minister of Communications, stating that the Merchant Steamship Company sailors requested equal treatment and double wages with the bureau staff due to the company's unfair treatment. Guo Waifeng stubbornly refused and threatened to resign, causing the sailors to be in a desperate situation, leading to unexpected events. The responsibility lies entirely with Commissioner Guo. The sailors are determined to fight for personality and justice. In addition to being determined to wait for the bureau to issue double wages, they can drive to various ports and continue their daily work as usual. There are no other actions. In addition, the "Jiangyu" ship is currently used for military purposes and urgently needs to be transported. In order to facilitate military affairs and support the government, colleagues decided to order the ship's employees to sail as usual. I hereby state the truth. The telegraph was reported. (The following is omitted)

Bilateral Consultation: At 7:00 PM yesterday, Du's residence called a meeting of representatives of sailors and stokers to Du's residence to consult with the two mediators, Du and Quan, on a solution. The representatives went around 7:00 PM. While reporters were drafting this manuscript, the two sides were still consulting. The result will be discussed and decided today.

Shipping Situation: The Merchant Steamship Company's suspension has lasted for three days. It is currently the peak season for cargo transport in the Yangtze River and the North and South Seas, resulting in huge losses in operations. Yesterday, the Sanbei Company took this opportunity to add the new ship "Songpu" to the Yangtze River route in order to intercept the cargo and passengers of the Merchant Steamship Company. Cargo and passengers in the North and South Seas were loaded by Taikoo and Jardine Matheson ships. Therefore, the "Fusheng," "Shuntian," and "Zhangzhou" ships had more cargo and passengers than usual yesterday.

Letter to the Municipal Government: Guo Waifeng, Commissioner of the General Administration Office of the Reorganization of the Merchant Steamship Company of the National Government, sent an official letter to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the sudden strike by the company's river and sea sailors on the 8th, citing the issue of year-end double wages, a total of twelve ships arriving at the port have been incited to join. Declarations have also been published in newspapers and presented to party and government agencies. However, the contents stated are inconsistent with the current situation and are absurd. The treatment of the company's sailors is more than twice that of the company's employees. Since the special commissioner was ordered to reorganize the company, the arrears of sailors' salaries have been paid for more than two months. Everything that can benefit the sailors has been done to the best of our ability. In addition to actively reforming currency treasures, we have also followed regulations and customs to care for all internal and external employees without any favoritism. However, the sailors disregarded national transportation and went on strike. Even after being advised to resume sailing, they turned a deaf ear. Although this is a dispute within the company, transportation is involved, and I am afraid it will affect local security. I hereby send a letter to your noble municipal government, requesting you to order the relevant departments to jointly find a way to mediate and quickly resolve the situation and resume sailing, in order to prevent future hidden dangers in the area. Public and private sectors will be grateful. Sincerely, Wu, Mayor of Shanghai Municipal Government; Guo Waifeng, Commissioner of the General Administration Office of the Reorganization of the Merchant Steamship Company of the National Government."

Advising to Resume Sailing: Guo Waifeng, Commissioner of the Merchant Steamship Company, issued a notice to all sailors on the river and sea ships yesterday, stating: "Regarding the fact that the company's river and sea sailors suddenly declared a strike and suspended sailing due to the issue of double wages and published a declaration and reported to party and government agencies, the contents listed are inconsistent with the current situation. It is even said that the special commissioner is used by others to oppress sailors. I was surprised after reading it. Since I was ordered to come to the bureau last May, the first thing I did was to request the National Government to cancel the bonus. The purpose of this is to seek internal and external balance and expect equal treatment. After approval, the bonus will be cancelled. The twentieth-year business department's cargo loading comparison still exceeds the regulations, but the bonus will be stopped from now on. The sailors are still using this as a reason to demand double wages, which is ignorant of the fact that the yellow flowers are tomorrow. In addition, during the previous Zhao Shou era, the salaries of sailors on each ship were in arrears, many for four or five months, and at least two or one month. The sailors' meals and miscellaneous expenses were issued with long-term checks, which were often difficult to cash when due, which affected the sailors' livelihoods. After I took over, I deeply sympathized with the sailors' situation and tried my best to find a way to solve the problem. I first actively raised and issued all the arrears of salaries for each month on each ship, regardless of the amount, and changed all the meals and miscellaneous expenses of each ship to cash. Everything that can benefit the sailors has been properly taken care of. I have done my best to love and protect the sailors. What is the oppression of the sailors? As for the fact that the bureau staff enjoys year-end double wages, but the sailors do not, which is considered a clear proof of unfair treatment, let alone the fact that the special commissioner handles this matter purely in accordance with old rules and takes into account industry practices, and I have no favoritism. Even just in terms of treatment, who is more or less, the bureau staff or the sailors, is difficult to say. For example, the upper-level sailors are provided with Western food, which costs 7,000 to 8,000 yuan per month. The lower-level sailors also increased the rice subsidy by 4 yuan per person per month last year. When the rice was cheap, it was not deducted. The total number of staff in the general office is the same as that of the upper-level sailors, and the monthly meal is only about 1,000 yuan. This is also a habit. The difference is so huge. Otherwise, the sailors are Chinese, and it is natural to provide Chinese food, which will save twice as much. In addition, sailors can ask for leave for illness, and the bureau will send a representative, who will be paid the original salary, and the representative must be paid separately. In recent years, sailors have asked for leave more often, and the bureau's losses may not be less than one month's double wages. However, the bureau staff mostly ask colleagues to handle their affairs, and there is no cost of sending a representative. In addition, medical care and compensation are stipulated by the Maritime Law, and there is no need to list them one by one. If you want to seek equality, then just reform the two matters of meals and leave, so that it is the same as the bureau staff. Do you want the sailors? The feet are long, and the inches are short. If you want to be fair, you must first reflect on yourself. I hope that all the sailors will not only hope for the one-month double wages of the bureau staff, but also think about the usual favoritism. You must be calm and peaceful, and there is nothing to compete for. In short, I have no intention to refuse the sailors' request for double pay, but it is not allowed to consider the precedents and the fairness of the treatment. It is not reasonable to allow it suddenly, and whether the current financial resources of the bureau can afford this additional huge expense is also known to all internal and external staff. The sailors only know that the bureau has a capital of 50 million yuan, but the estimated value is only more than 28 million taels, and they do not know that the annual debt interest is more than 2 million yuan. Every year, there has been a long-standing deficit, and it is difficult to support it. If you do not measure the bureau's difficulties, you will inevitably make excessive demands, which will consume more and more, and production will not increase. If the beams and rafters break, you will eventually be crushed. I am worried about the future. At this time of national crisis and when the goods are being shipped smoothly, each ship is fully loaded and sits in the river. The daily losses are immeasurable. If you understand the big picture, how can you make this? Resume classes and sailing immediately, and do not delay. I have always been fair and sincere in treating my subordinates. I hereby sincerely inform you, and I hope you will all abide by it."

Shanghai Sent Representatives to Beijing to Petition

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, representatives of various Fujian organizations hosted various local organizations at the Shanghai YMCA. Representatives from secondary schools' anti-Japanese national salvation joint associations, Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association representatives Wu Yu, Feng Yuxiang representative Wang Daoyu, and Fujian natives association in Shanghai and other 40+ organizations attended. Firstly, Chen Zhihao, Chairman of the delegation, reported, stating: "On the 2nd of this month, when Fuzhou students were conducting a national salvation propaganda in West Lake Park, the Japanese consul in Fujian, accompanied by the captain of the northbound warship, disguised themselves and tore up slogans and fired guns to demonstrate. Later, they were protected by the military police and left. However, they did not blame themselves and instead made serious representations to the provincial government. The next night (the 3rd), Japanese couple Mito Sanshio were killed in the Japanese Club residence. The place was heavily guarded, with military police standing. After this incident, the Japanese consul falsely accused the Chinese of the murder, causing a great disturbance, deploying troops and ships, and making unreasonable demands of five conditions, limiting the Fujian Provincial Government to respond within 24 hours. The provincial government succumbed and actually acknowledged it, causing the people's anger and resentment to be unable to extend. Therefore, they sent people to Shanghai to request assistance from all sectors." Then, Wu Mai, representative of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, and Wang Daoyu, representative of Feng Yuxiang, gave speeches in succession. Their words were impassioned and the whole audience was angry. Subsequently, three concrete measures were proposed by all sectors: 1) All sectors will convene a meeting immediately to send a telegram to the whole country to request assistance. 2) All sectors will request the central government to make serious representations to Japan. 3) All sectors will send representatives to Beijing to petition and severely punish the Fujian Provincial Government that is flattering foreigners and humiliating the country. The meeting ended at about 6:00 PM.

Ningbo Association Plans to Aid Compatriots in Japan

Since the outbreak of the Northeast issue, no less than thousands of overseas Chinese in Japan have lost their jobs and returned to their country. It has been heard that there are still 22 unemployed overseas Chinese in Japan from Wenzhou, Zhejiang, wandering from various parts of Kyushu, Japan, to Nagasaki. There are also 16 fishermen from Dinghai County who were shipwrecked and drifted to Japan, urgently awaiting repatriation. The directors of the Sanjiang Association in Nagasaki, Zichang and others, telegraphed the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, asking them to find ways to provide relief to avoid being stranded in a foreign land. After receiving the telegram, the association, in addition to forwarding a letter to the Wenzhou Association in Shanghai to find a solution, has already telegraphed the Sanjiang Association regarding the Ningbo fishermen, requesting them to advance funds to be sent back to their hometowns.

Dispute at Nisshin Cotton Mill

Failure to Pay Workers' Wages

The Nisshin First Cotton Mill in Gordon Road, Puxi, has been greatly affected by the boycott of Japanese goods in China, and its business has declined sharply, making it almost unsustainable. Therefore, it came up with the fantastic idea of arbitrarily oppressing and increasing the workload of a large number of workers, deducting wages, forcing the workers to resign and quit, and refusing to allow the workers to enter the factory to work yesterday afternoon, in order to achieve its goal of closing the factory. All wages, labor bonuses, etc. that the workers should have received were not paid, causing more than 2,000 workers in the factory to be extremely angry and are currently holding a general meeting to discuss countermeasures.

At 12:00 noon yesterday, the Chinese Business Administration Association held a meeting on the fourth floor of the Jianghai Customs to welcome Mr. Feng Huanzhang. Over 100 people attended, presided over by Kong Xiangxi, who said that Mr. Feng is not only an outstanding talent in China, but also an outstanding talent in the world. Feng then gave a speech, saying that listening to Mr. Kong just now, I felt infinitely emotional when I heard that your association is a professional research organization of scientific management. The corruption of Chinese national affairs lies in the lack of scientific management spirit. What is learned is often not what is used, and what is learned is not what is used. In the late Qing Dynasty, the acting official was omnipotent, and he was called flying all over the sky. What is the director? Supervisor? Director General? Platoon leader? None of them were managed by acting officials. As a result, the world of the Qing Dynasty was lost. Since the Republic of China, it has become the omnipotence of the military. What is the governor of the province? Hall chief? Committee member? Chairman? None of them are military tyrants occupying them. What did you ask him to learn? He learned the left, right, left, and right. What did you ask him to know? He knew how to drag a gun and count one, two, three, four, but he insisted on handling political affairs, holding a large group of laymen to impersonate experts, so how can national affairs not get worse and worse? I believe that why not find professional scientists to design and be responsible for the country in the future, then the future is very difficult, so I advocate that all management of the country in the future should be scientific. In short, it is to scientifically manage the country. I am a crude person who dropped out of school in his childhood, but I know that I have many things that are laymen and there are mistakes. Please give me your advice. Cao Yunxiang then gave a speech, saying that I personally saw Mr. Feng's soldiers helping the people to push cars and helping the people to pull cars when I was in Kaifeng Prefecture. This is a phenomenon that is not found in the whole of China, so training troops is Mr. Feng's expertise, which is well known. It will never be a layman. We hope that Mr. Feng will specialize in training troops for the country in the future. The troops trained by Mr. Feng will definitely be able to fight the Japanese, and they will definitely not take the policy of non-resistance. Jiang Hengyuan's speech was long and not recorded.

Wang Jingwei's Statement on Stopping Seeing Guests

It is reported that a letter came from Wang Gongguan's Secret Office on the 9th, saying that the recent reports in various Shanghai newspapers about Mr. Wang meeting guests are slightly inconsistent with the facts. During the interim of the fourth session of the first central provincial conference, Mr. Wang was unable to attend due to illness. There were many important issues that the committee members had to come to Shanghai to discuss with Mr. Wang in person. At that time, Mr. Wang spoke too much, which aggravated his illness. After this (after the end of the full meeting), he followed the doctor's advice and stopped seeing guests and focused on recuperating. The recent reports of talking with a certain public official for 30 minutes and talking with a certain public official for 50 minutes are not true. According to the doctor, in the shortest period of time, he can not only not see guests, but also not read newspapers, because only in this way can he have the possibility of recovering his health in a considerable period of time. Now I am afraid that the outside world does not understand the truth and is prone to misunderstandings. I hereby make a statement based on the facts and respectfully publish it in the newspapers, so as not to fail to welcome those who come to visit Mr. Wang. Wang Gong reported to the secretariat on the 9th.

Special News from the Aviation Industry

Qinghe Runs Aground: The Shanghai steamer Qinghe of Jardine Matheson's ship, this time went upstream to Junqing. On the 5th of this month, the ship was traveling above Wanxian. Due to the reduction of the river water, it ran aground. The hull was stranded on the reef, and the bottom of the ship was pierced, with two holes. The river water immediately flooded into the ship, and the goods were damaged. The shipowner temporarily plugged the holes with cement, drained the accumulated water, and reluctantly drove to Chongqing. Yesterday, the Shanghai office telegraphed the ship to unload the goods and then open to Shanghai for overhaul.

Taishun Fire: The Taishun ship of the Merchant Steamship Bureau was loading goods in Shanghai this time and planned to go to Beiyang, but the strike started just as the passengers and goods were loaded, so it was not successful. Hundreds of bales of cotton were loaded on the upper deck of the ship. Unexpectedly, a fire suddenly broke out. The fire spread very quickly for a while. Only when the fire broke through did the shipowner and others learn about it and immediately took leather straps to absorb water and shoot. The fire brigade also drove the dragons to help put out the fire. The fire was finally extinguished, burning several bales of cotton. The ship's hull was not affected, but there was a lot of water on the deck. The cause of the fire is unknown and is currently under investigation.

Appointment of Section Chiefs for Dredging Yu Tang

Regarding the dredging project of the Yu Tang River in Shanghai County, all procedures have been prepared by the River Works Office. It is now planned to implement the earth excavation during this sunny winter season. However, with the river stretching two hundred and ten li, it is difficult to effectively oversee the work. Therefore, following the method of recruiting labor for road construction, seventeen individuals with river works experience were selected from the dredging maps to serve as section chiefs, so as to direct the village chiefs in supervising the earthworkers' dredging, for the benefit of the river works. Sun Shiben, the director of the River Works General Office, submitted a list to the county government for appointment. Yesterday, County Magistrate Yan issued an order approving the request, and appointed Qiao Fu, Lu Zhaoxiang, Lu Mingru, Guo Jingfu, Ling Yengeng, Jiang Fengyi, and six others as section chiefs of the North Bridge River Works General Office. Yu Yuxiang, Cao Yazhou, Yang Rusheng, Chen Shen'an, and four others were appointed as section chiefs of the Tangwan Branch Office. Nie Qiaosheng, Zhang Zhongmei, Shen Zhicheng, Zhang Zhonghua, Xu Yuexiang, Wang Baren, Gu Baixiong, and seven others were appointed as section chiefs of the Maqiao Branch Office.

Representatives of the French Municipal Council Chinese Association Petitioned the Municipal Government Again Yesterday

Regarding the Dismissal of Chinese Staff by the Council

The French Municipal Council of this city implemented a staff reduction plan on December 2 last year, planning to dismiss 217 Chinese employees. Including the workers laid off in November, the total was 242. The Chinese Association of the Council sent representatives to the municipal government on December 8 to petition. After accepting the petition, the municipal government verbally negotiated with the French authorities and sent a letter to the Council to inquire. Many days have passed, but the Council has not yet replied, causing the case to remain unresolved. The Association again sent representatives Shen Caigeng, Yang Wugang, Sun Shanhai, Fan Agui, Gu Xigeng, and others to the municipal government yesterday to petition. The receiving secretary, Geng Jizhi, met with them and promised to send another letter to the French authorities to negotiate strictly. The result was extremely satisfactory.

The Datong Music Society Will Film a Sound Movie

A Precursor to the Westward Spread of National Music

The Datong Music Society of this port recently received an official letter from the Ministry of Education stating that the League of Nations had appointed experts to China to investigate the true state of cultural life, and intended to request the Society to perform national music and film it into a sound movie to promote it to various countries around the world. The Society convened all its members last Sunday afternoon to discuss the matter, and replied to the Ministry of Education, agreeing to do so. It also summoned members and experts from other locations to Shanghai to join the performance, totaling about fifty people. Preparations will be made for two weeks before filming. It is said that the content is quite extensive, including more than 160 kinds of ancient and modern musical instruments and 11 kinds of dance instruments, divided into two major categories: solo and ensemble, mostly high-quality works for public enjoyment. It is certain to create a unique style in world music and strive for a ray of glory for our inherent culture. In the future, if music and ritual flourish and the old system of the Grand Master of Music of the Zhou Dynasty can be restored, the future of national music will be immeasurable. According to Director Zheng of the Society, this initiative lacks neither talent nor musical instruments, but the funding issue is quite difficult due to the lack of a foundation.

Wang Tianming, the chief of staff of the tax police corps, concurrently served as the director of the Zhabei Military Police Corps Joint Office. Recently, the tax police corps was ordered to go to Songjiang and left Shanghai the day before yesterday. All duties as director have been resigned to the municipal government garrison headquarters to relieve responsibility. It has been approved, and Zhang Junsong, the commander of the Sixth Corps of the 78th Division and concurrently the commander of the Shanghai North China, has been appointed to succeed him.

First Landowners' Association in the Central District

Since the first public land release in the central district of Shanghai last July, the Engineering Bureau has been actively carrying out road construction projects. Former Mayor Zhang, in order to strengthen public trust and demonstrate fairness, issued a clear order on December 22 last year to establish a Construction Fund Management Committee for the central district area to manage funds and allocate expenditures, and also announced that landowners should elect two representatives as committee members. It is now known that the eleven landowners in the first land release have formed the first Landowners' Association in the central district and have elected the Bank of China (represented by Xia Pingfang) and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank (represented by Dong Chengdao) as representatives of the first landowners and submitted them to the municipal government for record. The newly appointed Mayor Wu has made a declaration that the construction of Greater Shanghai will be actively carried out so that various plans will be completed one by one, then the prosperity of the central district area must be realized soon, it can be asserted.

Record of the Xu-Xi Wedding

Xu Pei, the dean of the School of Commerce at Central University, and the famous Miss Xi Baozhen held their wedding ceremony at the Yipinxin Hotel at 5 pm yesterday. Xu has a wide circle of friends, and more than 500 people from the political, business, and academic circles came to congratulate him, including Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jilun, Fang Jiaobo, Yuan Ludun, Wang Jingqi, Xu Zazhen, Li Lishen, Chen Xing, Qi Zhi, Li Zhaosui, Wang Xianhua, Cao Lianglu, and others. During the wedding, Xu's elder brother, Xu Juntao, the director of the Municipal Education Bureau, officiated, and Yu Qiaqing was the witness. In the evening, a banquet was held at Yipinxin to entertain the Chinese and foreign guests, who gathered together until late at night, and then dispersed in joy.

Western Horse Racing Harms Farmers

Request to the County Government for Negotiation

The Westerners' paper-scattering horse racing was previously banned due to damage to farmland. Unexpectedly, recently, more than a hundred Western men and women rode horses from Shanghai, passing west through Qianliang Temple in the county, passing through Huajing Guan Port to the south, and turning north to Caoxing Town, returning from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road. These Westerners did not follow the roads, but arbitrarily galloped in the farmland, trampling on broad beans, rapeseed, wheat seedlings, etc., causing considerable damage. The county's Public Security Second Sub-bureau immediately dissuaded them to no avail. Therefore, Director Zhao reported the situation to the County National Government yesterday, requesting an investigation and negotiation.

Robbery on Pingjili Road Last Night

At about 10 o'clock last night, four robbers suddenly came to Shengda Pawnshop at No. 131, the intersection of Pingjili Road and Rue Lafayette in the French Concession. Three robbers held guns, and one robber closed the front door, forbidding anyone from making a sound and wantonly looting. After about an hour, they fled with their loot. After a detailed inspection, the lost items were estimated to be about 4,000 yuan. The owner then provided a list of lost items and reported it to the police station for investigation.

Appeal Against Excessive Extortion on Lime Boats

Several dozen tin gang boat owners, including Qian Ating and Qian Peirong, submitted a petition to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating that they transport first-class lime from various lime kilns in Yixing to Shanghai for sale. Unexpectedly, Xu Shengfang, Zhou Jinfang, Ma Shaoquan, and others initiated the Lime Transportation and Sales Association, and in the name of the association, they sent people to wharves such as Caojiadu and Tanziwan in western Shanghai to collect fees from lime boats at a rate of one-third of a dan (unit of weight), and forced them to only sell at business locations, depriving the boat owners of their freedom to sell. Because Qian Ating's boat did not pay the fee, the water patrol team was brought along to detain the boat owner's son, Qian Xuelin. Qian Peirong's boat had its oars, masts, and splints taken away. However, the association is organized in the name of a business, and its main body has nothing to do with the boat owners. The behavior is inevitably harassing and demanding. They request an investigation and release of the arrested person. Otherwise, dozens of ships will have to simultaneously request the bureau to maintain their livelihoods and resort to extremes. After receiving the petition, the bureau has consulted the Public Security Bureau for verification and handling.

Police Detective Arrests Two More Robbers

The home of Yong native Zhu Shende at No. 21 Chunyang Lane, Qiazibuzaitou, No. 4 Youheng Road, was invaded by five robbers at around 6:30 the night before last. Detective Zheng Huaili, No. 308 of the Jiaxing Road Police Station, who lived in the same house, fired a shot and wounded one robber, capturing him on the spot. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Detective Zheng went to his elder brother's place at No. 1174 near Sheng Road, Pingliang Road for lunch. Suddenly, he saw three people passing by outside the door, and he suddenly remembered that their faces resembled the robbers who had been in his house the night before. Therefore, he went out to stop them. Unexpectedly, the robbers were already alarmed. One of them, wearing a suit, took out a gun and tried to fire, but Zheng preemptively fired five shots, hitting and capturing two robbers. One robber took the opportunity to escape without a trace. When Zheng fired, Wang Xuanhao, an employee of the Tianyi Silk Factory, happened to be passing by. A stray bullet hit his left leg, and he went to Tongren Hospital for treatment. He was not seriously injured.

Dispute at the Kangfu Confectionery Factory

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Accepts Mediation

The Kangfu Confectionery Factory at Jiandao Bridge, Humin South Zhelu Road, Nanshi, was organized by Shi Xilin (28 years old) and others from Haining. It was opened in the spring of last year and specializes in selling machine-made chocolate candies. The business is still developing. The manager is Xie Songtang. On New Year's Eve last year, shareholder Shi Xilin suddenly came to the factory and announced that all workers in the hired machine room would work from 6:30 am to 8:30 pm. Manager Xie advised against it, believing that 14 hours of work per day was not in the interest of protecting laborers. Shi refused, and the two had a disagreement. Xie then resigned. When the workers heard about it, they rose up in opposition. According to the factory's custom, double pay is given every December. On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, Shi personally distributed the pay and asked the workers to sign. However, afterwards, he suddenly announced that all workers should leave their jobs because Shi added the words "Worker Retirement Money" to the list signed by the workers. Thereupon, the workers knew they had been fooled and refused to leave the factory. The shareholders used the "Worker Retirement Money" list as evidence of voluntary resignation. Therefore, yesterday morning, the factory sent the workers Zhou Delin and Zhou Jinsheng to the Second District Public Security Bureau for detention. When the workers learned of this, 13 machine workers submitted a detailed account of the incident, requesting assistance from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has accepted this mediation.

Fire at a Clothing Shop in Baxianqiao

At 9:25 last night, a fire suddenly broke out at Che Bingji Clothing Shop, No. 52 Yinyuli, Liselou Road, Baxianqiao, French Concession. It could not be contained and quickly spread. The Grand Bell and the Songshan Fire Brigade heard the alarm and drove to the scene to put out the fire. After about half an hour of spraying, the fire was completely extinguished, but only the three-story pavilion and the attic were destroyed, and the loss was still small.
